<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;2.02. Results of Operations and Financial Condition </p> <p style="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify"><span style="font-style:italic">The information in Item 2.02 of this Current Report, including the accompanying Exhibits 99.1 and 99.2, is being furnished and shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for the purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of Section&#160;18. The information in Item 2.02 of this Current Report shall not be incorporated by reference into any registration statement or other document filed pursuant to the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, regardless of any general incorporation language contained in such filing. </span></p> <p style="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Financial Results for the Quarter Ended March&#160;31, 2024 </span></p> <p style="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">On April&#160;30, 2024, PayPal Holdings, Inc. (&#8220;PayPal,&#8221; the &#8220;Company,&#8221; &#8220;we,&#8221; &#8220;us,&#8221; or &#8220;our&#8221;) issued a press release announcing its financial results for the quarter ended March&#160;31, 2024. A copy of the press release is furnished as Exhibit&#160;99.1 hereto and is incorporated by reference herein. </p> <p style="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Presentation of Historical <span style="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</span> Earnings per Share Pursuant to New Methodology </span></p> <p style="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">As previously announced on February&#160;7, 2024, beginning with the first quarter of 2024, PayPal Holdings, Inc. is modifying the presentation of its <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> results to include the impact of stock-based compensation expense and related employer payroll taxes.&#160;This modification is intended to enhance transparency and discipline as stock-based compensation expense is an integral part of our cost structure. We believe this new methodology will enhance investors&#8217; overall understanding of our operating performance. These changes have no impact on any of the Company&#8217;s previously reported U.S. GAAP results for any periods presented. Additionally, these changes have no impact on the Company&#8217;s previously reported free cash flows for any periods presented. </p> <p style="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">The following tables present the effects of the changes on the presentation of <span style="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</span> earnings per share (&#8220;EPS&#8221;) as reflected in the Company&#8217;s previous reports. </p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>EX-99.1</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE" STYLE="line-height:Normal">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right">Exhibit 99.1 </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g831310g0427012056228.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:13pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><FONT COLOR="#051735"><B>PayPal Reports First Quarter 2024 Results </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><FONT COLOR="#051735">San Jose, California <FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:SYMBOL">&#189;</FONT> April&nbsp;30, 2024
<FONT STYLE="FONT-FAMILY:SYMBOL">&#189;</FONT> NASDAQ: PYPL </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><FONT COLOR="#051735"><B>Q1&#146;24 revenue increased 9% to
$7.7&nbsp;billion; 10% on a currency-neutral basis (FXN) </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><FONT COLOR="#051735"><B>Q1&#146;24 GAAP EPS increased 18% to $0.83; <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> EPS increased 27% to $1.08 (based on new non-GAAP methodology as described below) </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">&#147;We delivered a solid set of results in Q1 and I&#146;m encouraged by the progress the team is making against PayPal&#146;s <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">go-forward</FONT> strategy and in strengthening our foundation. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">2024 remains a transition year and we are
focused on execution &#150; driving our key strategic initiatives, realizing cost savings, and reinvesting appropriately to position the company for consistent, high-quality profitable growth in the future.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><FONT COLOR="#1f285f"><B>Alex Chriss </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">President and CEO </P> <P STYLE="font-size:8pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="line-height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><FONT COLOR="#1f285f"><B>Q1&#146;24
Financial Results </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I>As announced on February&nbsp;7, 2024, the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
results are based on a new methodology that includes the impact of stock-based compensation (SBC) expense and related employer payroll taxes. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> results for 2023, 2022 and 2021 have been recast to
reflect this change. See Exhibit 99.2 of the Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K</FONT> filed on April&nbsp;30, 2024 for historical reconciliations. </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net revenues increased 9% to $7.7&nbsp;billion; 10% FXN. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:4pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Transaction margin dollars increased 4% to $3.5&nbsp;billion. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">PayPal Holdings, Inc. will host a conference call to discuss first quarter 2024 results at 8:30 a.m. Eastern Time today. A live webcast of the
conference call, together with a slide presentation that includes supplemental financial information and reconciliations of certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures to their most directly comparable GAAP measures, can be
accessed through the company&#146;s Investor Relations website at https://investor.pypl.com. In addition, an archive of the webcast will be accessible for 90 days through the same link. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><FONT COLOR="#1f285f"><B>About PayPal </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">PayPal has been revolutionizing commerce globally for more than 25 years. Creating innovative experiences that make moving money, selling, and
shopping simple, personalized, and secure, PayPal empowers consumers and businesses in approximately 200 markets to join and thrive in the global economy. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><FONT COLOR="#1f285f"><B>Presentation </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">All growth rates represent year-over-year comparisons, except as otherwise noted. FXN results are calculated by translating the current period
local currency results by the prior period exchange rate. FXN growth rates are calculated by comparing the current period FXN results with the prior period results, excluding the impact from hedging activities. All amounts in tables are presented in
U.S. dollars, rounded to the nearest million, except as otherwise noted. As a result, certain amounts and rates may not sum or recalculate using the rounded dollar amounts provided. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><FONT COLOR="#1f285f"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">This press release includes financial measures defined as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures&#148; by
the SEC including: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> earnings per diluted share, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating income, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating margin, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> effective tax rate, free cash flow, and adjusted free cash flow. For an explanation of the foregoing
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures, please see <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures of Financial Performance&#148; included in this press release. These measures may be different from <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures used by other companies. The presentation of this financial information, which is not prepared under any comprehensive set of accounting rules or principles, is not intended to be
considered in isolation of, or as a substitute for, the financial information prepared and presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP). For a reconciliation of these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
financial measures to the most directly comparable GAAP measures, see <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures of Financial Performance,&#148; &#147;Reconciliation of GAAP Operating Income to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Operating Income and GAAP Operating Margin to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Operating Margin,&#148; &#147;Reconciliation of GAAP Net Income (Loss) to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Net Income, GAAP Diluted EPS to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Diluted EPS and GAAP Effective Tax Rate to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Effective Tax Rate,&#148;
and &#147;Reconciliation of Operating Cash Flow to Free Cash Flow and Adjusted Free Cash Flow.&#148; </P>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><FONT COLOR="#243b81"><B>PayPal Holdings, Inc. </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><FONT COLOR="#243b81"><B>Unaudited Summary of Consolidated Net Revenues </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Our revenues are classified into the following two categories: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:9pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:9pt"><I>Transaction revenues</I>: Net transaction fees charged to merchants and consumers on a transaction basis
based on the Total Payment Volume (&#147;TPV&#148;) completed on our payments platform. Growth in TPV is directly impacted by the number of payment transactions that we enable on our payments platform. We generate additional revenue from merchants
and consumers: on transactions where we perform currency conversion, when we enable cross-border transactions (i.e., transactions where the merchant and consumer are in different countries), to facilitate the instant transfer of funds for our
customers from their PayPal or Venmo account to their bank account or debit card, to facilitate the purchase and sale of cryptocurrencies, as contractual compensation from sellers that violate our contractual terms (for example, through fraud or
counterfeiting), and other miscellaneous fees. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:9pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:9pt"><I>Revenues from other value added services</I>: Net revenues derived primarily from revenue earned through
partnerships, referral fees, subscription fees, gateway fees, and other services we provide to our merchants and consumers. We also earn revenues from interest and fees earned on our portfolio of loans receivable, and interest earned on certain
assets underlying customer balances. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Amounts in the table are rounded to the nearest million, except as otherwise noted. As a result, certain
amounts may not recalculate using the rounded amounts provided. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">(1) </SUP>An active account
is an account registered directly with PayPal or a platform access partner that has completed a transaction on our platform, not including gateway-exclusive transactions, within the past 12 months. A platform access partner is a third party whose
customers are provided access to PayPal&#146;s platform or services through such third party&#146;s login credentials, including individuals and entities that utilize Hyperwallet&#146;s payout capabilities. A user may register on our platform to
access different products and may register more than one account to access a product. Accordingly, a user may have more than one active account. The number of active accounts provides management with additional perspective on the overall scale of
our platform, but may not have a direct relationship to our operating results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">(2)
</SUP>Number of payment transactions is the total number of payments, net of payment reversals, successfully completed on our payments platform or enabled by PayPal via a partner payment solution, not including gateway-exclusive transactions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">(3) </SUP>Number of payment transactions per active account reflects the total number of payment
transactions within the previous <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">12-month</FONT> period, divided by active accounts at the end of the period. The number of payment transactions per active account provides management with insight into the average
number of times an account engages in payments activity on our payments platform in a given period. The number of times a consumer account or a merchant account transacts on our platform may vary significantly from the average number of payment
transactions per active account. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">(4)</SUP> TPV is the value of payments, net of payment
reversals, successfully completed&nbsp;on our payments platform or enabled by PayPal via a partner payment solution, not including gateway-exclusive transactions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">(5) </SUP>Transaction expense rate is transaction expense divided by TPV. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">(6) </SUP>Transaction and credit loss rate is transaction and credit losses divided by TPV. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">(7) </SUP>Transaction margin is net revenues less transaction expense and transaction and credit
losses, divided by net revenues. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:4pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><FONT COLOR="#243b81"><B>PayPal Holdings, Inc. </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><FONT COLOR="#243b81"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures of Financial Performance </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">To supplement the company&#146;s condensed consolidated financial statements presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting
principles, or GAAP, the company uses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures of certain components of financial performance. These <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures include
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> earnings per diluted share, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating income,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating margin, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> effective tax rate, free cash flow, and adjusted free cash flow. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">These <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures are not in accordance with, or an alternative to, measures prepared in
accordance with GAAP and may be different from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures used by other companies. In addition, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures are not based on any comprehensive set of
accounting rules or principles. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> measures have limitations in that they do not reflect all of the amounts associated with the company&#146;s results of operations as determined in accordance with GAAP.
These measures should be used to evaluate the company&#146;s results of operations only in conjunction with the corresponding GAAP measures. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Reconciliation of all <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures to the most directly comparable GAAP measures can be found in
the subsequent tables included in this press release. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">These <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures are provided to
enhance investors&#146; overall understanding of the company&#146;s current financial performance and its prospects for the future. Specifically, the company believes the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures provide useful
information to both management and investors by excluding certain expenses, gains and losses, as the case may be, that may not be indicative of its core operating results and business outlook. In addition, because the company has historically
reported certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> results to investors, the company believes that the inclusion of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures provides consistency in the company&#146;s financial
reporting. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">For its internal budgeting process, and as discussed further below, the company&#146;s management uses financial measures that
do not include amortization or impairment of acquired intangible assets, impairment of goodwill, restructuring-related charges, certain other gains, losses, benefits, or charges that are not indicative of the company&#146;s core operating results,
and the income taxes associated with the foregoing. In addition to the corresponding GAAP measures, the company&#146;s management also uses the foregoing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures in reviewing the financial results of
the company. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The company excludes the following items from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> earnings per diluted share, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating income, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating margin, and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> effective tax rate: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:8.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I>Amortization or impairment of acquired intangible
assets, impairment of goodwill, and transaction expenses from the acquisition or disposal of a business. </I>We incur amortization or impairment of acquired intangible assets and goodwill in connection with acquisitions and may incur significant
gains or losses or transactional expenses from the acquisition or disposal of a business and therefore exclude these amounts from our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. We exclude these items because management does not
believe they are reflective of our ongoing operating results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:8.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I>Restructuring.</I> These consist of expenses related to
workforce reduction and include employee severance and benefits costs, real estate and facilities charges, stock-based compensation expense, and other exit and disposal costs. The company excludes significant restructuring charges primarily because
management does not believe they are reflective of ongoing operating results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:8.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I>Gains and losses on strategic
investments</I>. The gains and losses we record on our strategic investments are tied to the performance of the companies that we invest in.&nbsp;We exclude such gains and losses in full because the operations of the investee and the related gains
and losses are not indicative of our ongoing operating results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:8.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I>Certain other significant gains, losses, benefits, or
charges that are not indicative of the company&#146;s core operating results.</I>&nbsp;These are significant gains, losses, benefits, or charges during a period that are the result of isolated events or transactions that have not occurred frequently
in the past and are not expected to occur regularly in the future.&nbsp;The company excludes these amounts from its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> results because management does not believe they are indicative of our current or
ongoing operating results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:8.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I>Tax effect of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments.</I> This
adjustment is made to present the amounts described above on an <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> basis consistent with the presentation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">Free cash flow represents operating cash flows less purchases of property and equipment. The company uses free cash flow as a liquidity
measure that provides useful information to management and investors about the amount of cash generated by the business after the purchases of property, buildings, and equipment, which can then be used to, among other things, invest in the
company&#146;s business, make strategic acquisitions and investments, and repurchase stock. A limitation of the utility of free cash flow as a measure of financial performance is that it does not represent the total increase or decrease in the
company&#146;s cash balance for the period. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8.5pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">In addition to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures discussed above,
the company also analyzes certain measures, including net revenues and operating expenses, on an <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">FX-neutral</FONT> basis to better measure the comparability of operating results between periods. The company believes
that changes in foreign currency exchange rates are not indicative of the company&#146;s operations and evaluating growth in net revenues and operating expenses on an <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">FX-neutral</FONT> basis provides an additional
meaningful and comparable assessment of these measures to both management and investors. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">FX-neutral</FONT> results are calculated by translating the current period&#146;s local currency results with the prior
period&#146;s exchange rate. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">FX-neutral</FONT> growth rates are calculated by comparing the current period&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">FX-neutral</FONT> results by the prior period&#146;s results,
excluding the impact from hedging activities. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">(1)</SUP> As announced on February 7, 2024, the Company&#146;s
non-GAAP results now include the impact of stock-based compensation expense and related employer payroll taxes. Prior period non-GAAP results have been recast to reflect this change. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">(2)</SUP> Beginning in 2024, restructuring includes any stock-based compensation associated with
the restructuring activities. The three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2024 include $38&nbsp;million of stock-based compensation expense. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><SUP
STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">(3)</SUP> The three months ended March&nbsp;31, 2023 includes $39&nbsp;million in asset impairment charges for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">right-of-use</FONT></FONT>
lease assets and related leasehold improvements in conjunction with exiting certain leased properties and a loss of $8&nbsp;million from the designation of an owned property as held for sale. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I>As announced on February&nbsp;7, 2024, the impact of stock-based compensation expense and
related employer payroll taxes are now included in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> results. </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I>The below
reconciliation shows first quarter 2024 and 2023 results under the prior methodology, which does not include the impact of stock-based compensation expense and related employer payroll taxes, to provide a comparable basis for the first quarter 2024
guidance which was provided on the same date. </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify"><I>Going forward, all <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> results and
guidance will include the impact of stock-based compensation expense and related employer payroll taxes and we will not provide reconciliations based on the prior methodology. </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><FONT COLOR="#243b81"><B>Reconciliation of GAAP Net Income (Loss) to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Net Income and GAAP
